{"answers": ["Middle Eastern alchemy"], "model_answer": "The term \"spirits\" for alcohol originated from Middle Eastern alchemy. In the Middle East, alchemists were more concerned with medical elixirs than with transmuting lead into gold. The vapor given off and collected during an alchemical process (as with distillation of alcohol) was called a spirit of the original material. This term was later adopted in Europe, where it referred to the distilled essence of wine, and eventually became a general term for any distilled beverage."}
